I've uploaded a code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
[BUG] Lambda: UpdateFunctionCode missing LastUpdateStatus in response (breaks Terraform re-apply)
## Service

Lambda

## AWS API Action

`UpdateFunctionCode` + `GetFunction` (polling for completion)

## Expected behavior

After `UpdateFunctionCode`, the Terraform AWS provider polls `GetFunction` waiting for `LastUpdateStatus` to become `"Successful"`. Real AWS returns this field in `GetFunction` and `GetFunctionConfiguration` responses.

## Actual behavior

Floci's `GetFunction` response does not include `LastUpdateStatus` (or returns an empty string). Terraform's state waiter sees `""` instead of `"Successful"` and fails:

```
Error: updating Lambda Function (my-function) code: waiting for completion:
unexpected state '', wanted target 'Successful'. last error:
```

This only occurs on **re-apply** (updating an existing Lambda), not on initial creation.

## Reproduction

```bash
docker run -d -p 4566:4566 hectorvent/floci:1.5.3

# Create a Lambda
aws --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566 lambda create-function \
  --function-name test-func --runtime provided.al2 \
  --handler bootstrap --role arn:aws:iam::000000000000:role/test \
  --zip-file fileb://package.zip

# Update the code (simulating Terraform re-apply)
aws --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566 lambda update-function-code \
  --function-name test-func --zip-file fileb://package.zip

# Check GetFunction response
aws --endpoint-url http://localhost:4566 lambda get-function \
  --function-name test-func --query 'Configuration.LastUpdateStatus'
# → Returns null instead of "Successful"
```

### Terraform context

On second `terraform apply`, Terraform detects a code hash change and calls `UpdateFunctionCode`, then polls `GetFunction` for `LastUpdateStatus == "Successful"`.

## Impact

- First `terraform apply` succeeds (create path)
- Second `terraform apply` fails for all Lambda functions (update path)
- Affects any repo with Lambdas when running apply more than once

## Suggested fix

Include `LastUpdateStatus: "Successful"` and `LastUpdateStatusReason: "The function was successfully updated"` in `GetFunction` / `GetFunctionConfiguration` responses.

## Environment

- Floci: 1.5.3
- Terraform AWS provider: >= 5.17.0

</pr_description>

    13	import jakarta.inject.Inject;
    14	import jakarta.ws.rs.Consumes;
    15	import jakarta.ws.rs.DELETE;
    16	import jakarta.ws.rs.GET;
    17	import jakarta.ws.rs.POST;
    18	import jakarta.ws.rs.PUT;
    19	import jakarta.ws.rs.Path;
    20	import jakarta.ws.rs.PathParam;
    21	import jakarta.ws.rs.Produces;
    22	import jakarta.ws.rs.QueryParam;
    23	import jakarta.ws.rs.core.Context;
    24	import jakarta.ws.rs.core.HttpHeaders;
    25	import jakarta.ws.rs.core.MediaType;
    26	import jakarta.ws.rs.core.Response;
    27	import org.jboss.logging.Logger;
    28	
    29	import java.util.List;
    30	import java.util.Map;
    31	
    32	/**
    33	 * AWS Lambda API REST endpoints.
    34	 * All endpoints are under /2015-03-31 matching the AWS Lambda API version.
    35	 */
    36	@Path("/2015-03-31")
    37	@Produces(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
    38	@Consumes(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON)
    39	public class LambdaController {
    40	
    41	    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(LambdaController.class);
    42	
    43	    private final LambdaService lambdaService;
    44	    private final RegionResolver regionResolver;
    45	    private final ObjectMapper objectMapper;
    46	
    47	    @Inject
    48	    public LambdaController(LambdaService lambdaService, RegionResolver regionResolver, ObjectMapper objectMapper) {
    49	        this.lambdaService = lambdaService;
    50	        this.regionResolver = regionResolver;
    51	        this.objectMapper = objectMapper;
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    // ──────────────────────────── CreateFunction ────────────────────────────
    55	
    56	    @POST
    57	    @Path("/functions")
    58	    public Response createFunction(@Context HttpHeaders headers, String body) {
    59	        String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(headers);
    60	        try {
    61	            @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
    62	            Map<String, Object> request = objectMapper.readValue(body, Map.class);
    63	            LambdaFunction fn = lambdaService.createFunction(region, request);
    64	            return Response.status(201)
    65	                    .entity(buildFunctionConfiguration(fn))
    66	                    .build();
    67	        } catch (AwsException e) {
    68	            throw e;
    69	        } catch (Exception e) {
    70	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException", e.getMessage(), 400);
    71	        }
    72	    }
    73	
    74	    // ──────────────────────────── GetFunction ────────────────────────────
    75	
    76	    @GET
    77	    @Path("/functions/{functionName}")
    78	    public Response getFunction(@Context HttpHeaders headers,
    79	                                @PathParam("functionName") String functionName) {
    80	        String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(headers);
    81	        LambdaFunction fn = lambdaService.getFunction(region, functionName);
    82	
    83	        ObjectNode root = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
    84	        root.set("Configuration", objectMapper.valueToTree(buildFunctionConfiguration(fn)));
    85	        ObjectNode code = root.putObject("Code");
    86	        if ("Image".equals(fn.getPackageType()) && fn.getImageUri() != null) {
    87	            code.put("RepositoryType", "ECR");
    88	            code.put("ImageUri", fn.getImageUri());
    89	            code.put("ResolvedImageUri", fn.getImageUri());
    90	        } else {
    91	            code.put("Location", "https://awslambda-" + region + "-tasks.s3." + region
    92	                    + ".amazonaws.com/" + fn.getFunctionName());
    93	            code.put("RepositoryType", "S3");
    94	        }
    95	
    96	        return Response.ok(root).build();
    97	    }
    98	
    99	    // ──────────────────────────── ListFunctions ────────────────────────────
   100	
   101	    @GET
   102	    @Path("/functions")
   103	    public Response listFunctions(@Context HttpHeaders headers) {
   104	        String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(headers);
   105	        List<LambdaFunction> functions = lambdaService.listFunctions(region);
   106	
   107	        ObjectNode root = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   108	        ArrayNode items = root.putArray("Functions");
   109	        for (LambdaFunction fn : functions) {
   110	            items.add(objectMapper.valueToTree(buildFunctionConfiguration(fn)));
   111	        }
   112	        return Response.ok(root).build();
   113	    }
   114	
   115	    // ──────────────────────────── GetFunctionConfiguration ────────────────────────────
   116	
   117	    @GET
   118	    @Path("/functions/{functionName}/configuration")
   119	    public Response getFunctionConfiguration(@Context HttpHeaders headers,
   120	                                              @PathParam("functionName") String functionName) {
   121	        String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(headers);
   122	        LambdaFunction fn = lambdaService.getFunction(region, functionName);
   123	        return Response.ok(buildFunctionConfiguration(fn)).build();
   124	    }

   129	    @Path("/functions/{functionName}/code")
   130	    public Response updateFunctionCode(@Context HttpHeaders headers,
   131	                                       @PathParam("functionName") String functionName,
   132	                                       String body) {
   133	        String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(headers);
   134	        try {
   135	            @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   136	            Map<String, Object> request = objectMapper.readValue(body, Map.class);
   137	            LambdaFunction fn = lambdaService.updateFunctionCode(region, functionName, request);
   138	            return Response.ok(buildFunctionConfiguration(fn)).build();
   139	        } catch (AwsException e) {
   140	            throw e;
   141	        } catch (Exception e) {
   142	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException", e.getMessage(), 400);
   143	        }
   144	    }
   145	
   146	    // ──────────────────────────── DeleteFunction ────────────────────────────
   147	
   148	    @DELETE
   149	    @Path("/functions/{functionName}")
   150	    public Response deleteFunction(@Context HttpHeaders headers,
   151	                                   @PathParam("functionName") String functionName) {
   152	        String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(headers);
   153	        lambdaService.deleteFunction(region, functionName);
   154	        return Response.noContent().build();
   155	    }
   156	
   157	    // ──────────────────────────── GetFunctionCodeSigningConfig ────────────────────────────
   158	
   159	    @GET
   160	    @Path("/functions/{functionName}/code-signing-config")
   161	    public Response getFunctionCodeSigningConfig(@Context HttpHeaders headers,
   162	                                                  @PathParam("functionName") String functionName) {
   163	        String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(headers);
   164	        // Verify the function exists
   165	        lambdaService.getFunction(region, functionName);
   166	        // Return empty code signing config — floci does not enforce code signing
   167	        ObjectNode root = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   168	        root.put("CodeSigningConfigArn", "");
   169	        root.put("FunctionName", functionName);
   170	        return Response.ok(root).build();
   171	    }
   172	
   173	    // ──────────────────────────── Invoke ────────────────────────────
   174	
   175	    @POST
   176	    @Path("/functions/{functionName}/invocations")
   177	    @Consumes(MediaType.WILDCARD)
   178	    public Response invoke(@Context HttpHeaders headers,
   179	                           @PathParam("functionName") String functionName,
   180	                           byte[] payload) {
   181	        String region = regionResolver.resolveRegion(headers);
   182	        String invocationTypeHeader = headers.getHeaderString("X-Amz-Invocation-Type");
   183	        InvocationType type = InvocationType.parse(invocationTypeHeader);
   184	
   185	        InvokeResult result = lambdaService.invoke(region, functionName, payload, type);
   186	
   187	        Response.ResponseBuilder builder = Response.status(result.getStatusCode());
   188	
   189	        if (result.getFunctionError() != null) {
   190	            builder.header("X-Amz-Function-Error", result.getFunctionError());
   191	        }
   192	        if (result.getLogResult() != null) {
   193	            builder.header("X-Amz-Log-Result", result.getLogResult());
   194	        }
   195	        builder.header("X-Amz-Executed-Version", "$LATEST");
   196	        builder.header("X-Amz-Request-Id", result.getRequestId());
   197	
   198	        if (result.getPayload() != null && result.getPayload().length > 0) {
   199	            builder.entity(result.getPayload())
   200	                    .type(MediaType.APPLICATION_JSON);
   201	        }
   202	
   203	        return builder.build();
   204	    }
   205

   220	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException", e.getMessage(), 400);

   450	
   451	    private Map<String, Object> buildAliasResponse(LambdaAlias alias) {
   452	        ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   453	        node.put("Name", alias.getName());
   454	        node.put("FunctionVersion", alias.getFunctionVersion() != null ? alias.getFunctionVersion() : "$LATEST");
   455	        node.put("AliasArn", alias.getAliasArn());
   456	        if (alias.getDescription() != null) node.put("Description", alias.getDescription());
   457	        node.put("RevisionId", alias.getRevisionId());
   458	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   459	        Map<String, Object> result = objectMapper.convertValue(node, Map.class);
   460	        return result;
   461	    }
   462	
   463	    private Map<String, Object> buildFunctionConfiguration(LambdaFunction fn) {
   464	        ObjectNode node = objectMapper.createObjectNode();
   465	        node.put("FunctionName", fn.getFunctionName());
   466	        node.put("FunctionArn", fn.getFunctionArn());
   467	        if (fn.getRuntime() != null) node.put("Runtime", fn.getRuntime());
   468	        node.put("Role", fn.getRole());
   469	        node.put("Handler", fn.getHandler());
   470	        if (fn.getDescription() != null) node.put("Description", fn.getDescription());
   471	        node.put("Timeout", fn.getTimeout());
   472	        node.put("MemorySize", fn.getMemorySize());
   473	        node.put("State", fn.getState());
   474	        if (fn.getStateReason() != null) node.put("StateReason", fn.getStateReason());
   475	        if (fn.getStateReasonCode() != null) node.put("StateReasonCode", fn.getStateReasonCode());
   476	        node.put("CodeSize", fn.getCodeSizeBytes());
   477	        node.put("PackageType", fn.getPackageType());
   478	        if (fn.getImageUri() != null) node.put("ImageUri", fn.getImageUri());
   479	        node.put("LastModified", String.valueOf(fn.getLastModified()));
   480	        node.put("RevisionId", fn.getRevisionId());
   481	        node.put("Version", fn.getVersion());
   482	
   483	        if (fn.getEnvironment() != null && !fn.getEnvironment().isEmpty()) {
   484	            ObjectNode envNode = node.putObject("Environment");
   485	            ObjectNode vars = envNode.putObject("Variables");
   486	            fn.getEnvironment().forEach(vars::put);
   487	        }
   488	
   489	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   490	        Map<String, Object> result = objectMapper.convertValue(node, Map.class);
   491	        return result;
   492	    }

   138	    /** Package-private accessor for tests that want to assert limiter state directly. */
   139	    LambdaConcurrencyLimiter concurrencyLimiter() {
   140	        return concurrencyLimiter;
   141	    }
   142	
   143	    /**
   144	     * Rehydrates reserved concurrency into the limiter from persisted function state.
   145	     * Without this, restarts leave {@code totalReserved()=0} and allow validatePut /
   146	     * unreserved-pool sizing to drift until each function is re-Put.
   147	     */
   148	    @PostConstruct
   149	    void rehydrateConcurrency() {
   150	        if (concurrencyLimiter == null) {
   151	            return;
   152	        }
   153	        int count = 0;
   154	        for (LambdaFunction fn : functionStore.listAll()) {
   155	            // Reserved concurrency is a function-level property; published
   156	            // versions share the $LATEST record's value. Skip non-$LATEST
   157	            // entries to avoid double-counting into totalReserved().
   158	            if (!"$LATEST".equals(fn.getVersion())) {
   159	                continue;
   160	            }
   161	            Integer reserved = fn.getReservedConcurrentExecutions();
   162	            if (reserved != null) {
   163	                concurrencyLimiter.setReserved(fn.getFunctionArn(), reserved);
   164	                count++;
   165	            }
   166	        }
   167	        if (count > 0) {
   168	            LOG.infov("Restored reserved concurrency for {0} function(s)", count);
   169	        }
   170	    }

   172	    public LambdaFunction createFunction(String region, Map<String, Object> request) {
   173	        String functionName = (String) request.get("FunctionName");
   174	        String role = (String) request.get("Role");
   175	        String handler = (String) request.get("Handler");
   176	        String runtime = (String) request.get("Runtime");
   177	        String packageType = request.getOrDefault("PackageType", "Zip").toString();
   178	        String description = (String) request.get("Description");
   179	        int timeout = toInt(request.get("Timeout"), config != null ? config.services().lambda().defaultTimeoutSeconds() : 3);
   180	        int memorySize = toInt(request.get("MemorySize"), config != null ? config.services().lambda().defaultMemoryMb() : 128);
   181	
   182	        if (functionName == null || functionName.isBlank()) {
   183	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException", "FunctionName is required", 400);
   184	        }
   185	        // Accept bare name, partial ARN, or full ARN. Normalize to the short
   186	        // name so duplicate detection works regardless of which form the
   187	        // caller supplies across successive calls.
   188	        functionName = canonicalFunctionName(region, functionName);
   189	        if (role == null || role.isBlank()) {
   190	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException", "Role is required", 400);
   191	        }
   192	        if ("Zip".equals(packageType) && (handler == null || handler.isBlank())) {
   193	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException", "Handler is required", 400);
   194	        }
   195	        if ("Zip".equals(packageType) && (runtime == null || runtime.isBlank())) {
   196	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException", "Runtime is required for Zip package type", 400);
   197	        }
   198	
   199	        if (functionStore.get(region, functionName).isPresent()) {
   200	            throw new AwsException("ResourceConflictException",
   201	                    "Function already exist: " + functionName, 409);
   202	        }
   203	
   204	        LambdaFunction fn = new LambdaFunction();
   205	        fn.setFunctionName(functionName);
   206	        fn.setFunctionArn(regionResolver.buildArn("lambda", region, "function:" + functionName));
   207	        fn.setRuntime(runtime);
   208	        fn.setRole(role);
   209	        fn.setHandler(handler);
   210	        fn.setDescription(description);
   211	        fn.setTimeout(timeout);
   212	        fn.setMemorySize(memorySize);
   213	        fn.setPackageType(packageType);
   214	        fn.setState("Active");
   215	        fn.setLastModified(System.currentTimeMillis());
   216	        fn.setRevisionId(UUID.randomUUID().toString());
   217	
   218	        // Handle environment variables
   219	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   220	        Map<String, Object> envBlock = (Map<String, Object>) request.get("Environment");
   221	        if (envBlock != null) {
   222	            @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   223	            Map<String, String> vars = (Map<String, String>) envBlock.get("Variables");
   224	            if (vars != null) fn.setEnvironment(vars);
   225	        }
   226	
   227	        // Handle tags
   228	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   229	        Map<String, String> tags = (Map<String, String>) request.get("Tags");
   230	        if (tags != null) fn.setTags(tags);
   231	
   232	        // Handle code deployment
   233	        @SuppressWarnings("unchecked")
   234	        Map<String, Object> code = (Map<String, Object>) request.get("Code");
   235	        if (code != null) {
   236	            String imageUri = (String) code.get("ImageUri");
   237	            if (imageUri != null) {
   238	                fn.setImageUri(imageUri);
   239	            }
   240	            String zipFileBase64 = (String) code.get("ZipFile");
   241	            if (zipFileBase64 != null) {
   242	                extractZipCode(fn, zipFileBase64);
   243	            }
   244	            String s3Bucket = (String) code.get("S3Bucket");
   245	            String s3Key = (String) code.get("S3Key");
   246	            if (s3Bucket != null && s3Key != null) {
   247	                extractZipCodeFromS3(fn, s3Bucket, s3Key);
   248	            }
   249	        }
   250	
   251	        functionStore.save(region, fn);
   252	        LOG.infov("Created Lambda function: {0} in region {1}", functionName, region);
   253	        return fn;
   254	    }

   260	                        "Function not found: " + functionName, 404));

   256	    public LambdaFunction getFunction(String region, String functionName) {

   262	
   263	    /**
   264	     * Resolves a {@code FunctionName} path parameter (bare name, partial ARN,
   265	     * or full ARN, with optional {@code :qualifier}) to its canonical short
   266	     * name, enforcing a region match when the input is a full ARN.
   267	     */
   268	    String canonicalFunctionName(String region, String functionName) {
   269	        LambdaArnUtils.ResolvedFunctionRef ref = LambdaArnUtils.resolve(functionName);
   270	        enforceRegion(region, ref);
   271	        return ref.name();
   272	    }
   273	
   274	    /**
   275	     * Resolves a {@code FunctionName} path parameter and reconciles any
   276	     * embedded qualifier with an explicit {@code ?Qualifier=} query-string
   277	     * value, enforcing region match when the input is a full ARN.
   278	     */
   279	    LambdaArnUtils.ResolvedFunctionRef resolveWithRegion(String region, String functionName, String queryQualifier) {
   280	        LambdaArnUtils.ResolvedFunctionRef ref = LambdaArnUtils.resolveWithQualifier(functionName, queryQualifier);
   281	        enforceRegion(region, ref);
   282	        return ref;
   283	    }
   284	
   285	    private void enforceRegion(String region, LambdaArnUtils.ResolvedFunctionRef ref) {
   286	        if (ref.region() != null && !ref.region().equals(region)) {
   287	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException",
   288	                    "Region '" + ref.region() + "' in ARN does not match request region '" + region + "'", 400);
   289	        }
   290	    }

   307	        }
   308	        if (imageUri != null) {
   309	            fn.setImageUri(imageUri);
   310	        }
   311	        if (s3Bucket != null && s3Key != null) {
   312	            extractZipCodeFromS3(fn, s3Bucket, s3Key);
   313	        }
   314	
   315	        fn.setLastModified(System.currentTimeMillis());
   316	        fn.setRevisionId(UUID.randomUUID().toString());
   317	
   318	        // Drain warm containers — they have stale code mounted
   319	        warmPool.drainFunction(functionName);
   320	
   321	        functionStore.save(region, fn);
   322	        LOG.infov("Updated code for function: {0}", functionName);
   323	        return fn;
   324	    }
   325	
   326	    public void deleteFunction(String region, String functionName) {
   327	        LambdaFunction fn = getFunction(region, functionName); // throws 404 if not found
   328	        functionName = fn.getFunctionName();
   329	        String arn = fn.getFunctionArn();
   330	        warmPool.drainFunction(functionName);
   331	        // Take the same per-function lock used by Put/DeleteFunctionConcurrency
   332	        // so a concurrent concurrency mutation cannot interleave with the
   333	        // limiter reset and store delete and leave the two views out of sync.
   334	        // The lock entry itself stays in the map after the delete: removing it
   335	        // could race with another thread already synchronized on the same
   336	        // object, letting a follow-up request allocate a fresh lock and run
   337	        // in parallel — the very serialization this map exists to prevent.
   338	        synchronized (lockForConcurrencyOp(arn)) {
   339	            if (concurrencyLimiter != null) {
   340	                concurrencyLimiter.reset(arn);
   341	            }
   342	            codeStore.delete(functionName);
   343	            functionStore.delete(region, functionName);
   344	        }
   345	        LOG.infov("Deleted Lambda function: {0}", functionName);
   346	    }
   347	
   348	    public InvokeResult invoke(String region, String functionName, byte[] payload, InvocationType type) {
   349	        LambdaFunction fn = getFunction(region, functionName);
   350	        return executorService.invoke(fn, payload, type);
   351	    }
   352	
   353	    // ──────────────────────────── Event Source Mapping (SQS) ────────────────────────────
   354	
   355	    public EventSourceMapping createEventSourceMapping(String region, Map<String, Object> request) {
   356	        String functionName = (String) request.get("FunctionName");
   357	        String eventSourceArn = (String) request.get("EventSourceArn");
   358	
   359	        if (functionName == null || functionName.isBlank()) {
   360	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException", "FunctionName is required", 400);
   361	        }
   362	        if (eventSourceArn == null || eventSourceArn.isBlank()) {
   363	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException", "EventSourceArn is required", 400);
   364	        }
   365	        if (!eventSourceArn.contains(":sqs:") && !eventSourceArn.contains(":kinesis:")
   366	                && !eventSourceArn.contains(":dynamodb:")) {
   367	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException",
   368	                    "Only SQS, Kinesis, and DynamoDB Streams event sources are supported.", 400);
   369	        }
   370	
   371	        // Resolve function — supports bare name, partial ARN, or full ARN
   372	        LambdaArnUtils.ResolvedFunctionRef fnRef = LambdaArnUtils.resolve(functionName);
   373	        String resolvedName = fnRef.name();
   374	
   375	        // Extract region from the event source ARN (parts[3] for all supported ARN formats)
   376	        String resolvedRegion;
   377	        if (eventSourceArn.contains(":sqs:")) {
   378	            resolvedRegion = SqsEventSourcePoller.regionFromArn(eventSourceArn);
   379	        } else {
   380	            // arn:aws:kinesis:region:... or arn:aws:dynamodb:region:...
   381	            String[] parts = eventSourceArn.split(":");
   382	            resolvedRegion = parts.length > 3 ? parts[3] : region;
   383	        }
   384	
   385	        // If the caller supplied a full function ARN, its region must agree
   386	        // with the region derived from the event source ARN. Otherwise we'd
   387	        // silently bind a different-region function of the same name.
   388	        if (fnRef.region() != null && !fnRef.region().equals(resolvedRegion)) {
   389	            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException",
   390	                    "Function ARN region '" + fnRef.region() + "' does not match event source region '" + resolvedRegion + "'", 400);

    private Object lockForConcurrencyOp(String functionArn) {

    public LambdaFunction getFunctionByUrlId(String urlId) {
        return functionStore.getByUrlId(urlId)
                .orElseThrow(() -> new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException", "Function not found for URL ID: " + urlId, 404));
    }

    public Object getTargetByUrlId(String urlId) {
        Optional<LambdaFunction> fn = functionStore.getByUrlId(urlId);
        if (fn.isPresent()) {
            return fn.get();
        }
        if (aliasStore != null) {
            Optional<LambdaAlias> alias = aliasStore.getByUrlId(urlId);
            if (alias.isPresent()) {
                return alias.get();
            }
        }
        throw new AwsException("ResourceNotFoundException", "No Lambda found for URL ID: " + urlId, 404);
    }

    private String[] toStringArray(Object obj) {
        if (obj instanceof List<?> list) {
            return list.stream().map(Object::toString).toArray(String[]::new);
        }
        return null;
    }

    private void extractZipCode(LambdaFunction fn, String zipFileBase64) {
        byte[] zipBytes = Base64.getDecoder().decode(zipFileBase64);
        Path codePath = codeStore.getCodePath(fn.getFunctionName());
        try {
            zipExtractor.extractTo(zipBytes, codePath);
            fn.setCodeLocalPath(codePath.toAbsolutePath().normalize().toString());
            fn.setCodeSizeBytes(zipBytes.length);

            // For file-based runtimes, verify handler file exists (skip Java and .NET which use different handler formats)
            if (fn.getRuntime() != null && !fn.getRuntime().startsWith("java") && !fn.getRuntime().startsWith("dotnet")) {
                String handlerFile = fn.getHandler().split("\\.")[0];
                boolean found = Files.walk(codePath)
                        .filter(Files::isRegularFile)
                        .anyMatch(p -> {
                            String relative = codePath.relativize(p).toString();
                            String withoutExt = relative.contains(".")
                                    ? relative.substring(0, relative.lastIndexOf('.'))
                                    : relative;
                            return withoutExt.equals(handlerFile);
                        });
                if (!found) {
                    throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException",
                            "Handler file '" + handlerFile + "' not found in deployment package", 400);
                }
            }
        } catch (AwsException e) {
            throw e;
        } catch (IOException e) {
            throw new AwsException("InvalidParameterValueException",
                    "Failed to extract deployment package: " + e.getMessage(), 400);
        }
    }

    private void extractZipCodeFromS3(LambdaFunction fn, String s3Bucket, String s3Key) {

package io.github.hectorvent.floci.services.lambda.zip;

import jakarta.enterprise.context.ApplicationScoped;
import org.jboss.logging.Logger;

import java.io.ByteArrayInputStream;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.io.OutputStream;
import java.nio.file.Files;
import java.nio.file.Path;
import java.util.zip.ZipEntry;
import java.util.zip.ZipInputStream;

/**
 * Extracts ZIP bytes to a target directory.
 * Guards against path traversal attacks by validating entry names.
 */
@ApplicationScoped
public class ZipExtractor {

    private static final Logger LOG = Logger.getLogger(ZipExtractor.class);

    public void extractTo(byte[] zipBytes, Path targetDir) throws IOException {
        // Resolve to absolute path so that normalize() on entry paths stays comparable
        Path absTarget = targetDir.toAbsolutePath().normalize();
        Files.createDirectories(absTarget);

        try (ZipInputStream zis = new ZipInputStream(new ByteArrayInputStream(zipBytes))) {
            ZipEntry entry;
            while ((entry = zis.getNextEntry()) != null) {
                String entryName = entry.getName();

                // Security: prevent path traversal
                if (entryName.contains("..") || entryName.startsWith("/")) {
                    LOG.warnv("Skipping suspicious ZIP entry: {0}", entryName);
                    zis.closeEntry();
                    continue;
                }

                Path targetPath = absTarget.resolve(entryName).normalize();
                if (!targetPath.startsWith(absTarget)) {
                    LOG.warnv("Skipping out-of-bounds ZIP entry: {0}", entryName);
                    zis.closeEntry();
                    continue;
                }

                if (entry.isDirectory()) {
                    Files.createDirectories(targetPath);
                } else {
                    Files.createDirectories(targetPath.getParent());
                    try (OutputStream out = Files.newOutputStream(targetPath)) {
                        zis.transferTo(out);
                    }
                }
                zis.closeEntry();
            }
        }

        LOG.debugv("Extracted ZIP to: {0}", absTarget);
    }
}

    10	
    11	@ApplicationScoped
    12	public class RegionResolver {
    13	
    14	    // Matches: Credential=AKID/20260215/us-west-2/s3/aws4_request
    15	    private static final Pattern CREDENTIAL_REGION_PATTERN =
    16	            Pattern.compile("Credential=\\S+/\\d{8}/([^/]+)/");
    17	
    18	    private final String defaultRegion;
    19	    private final String defaultAccountId;
    20	
    21	    @Inject
    22	    public RegionResolver(EmulatorConfig config) {
    23	        this(config.defaultRegion(), config.defaultAccountId());
    24	    }
    25	
    26	    public RegionResolver(String defaultRegion, String defaultAccountId) {
    27	        this.defaultRegion = defaultRegion;
    28	        this.defaultAccountId = defaultAccountId;
    29	    }
    30	
    31	    public String resolveRegion(HttpHeaders headers) {
    32	        if (headers == null) {
    33	            return defaultRegion;
    34	        }
    35	        String auth = headers.getHeaderString("Authorization");
    36	        if (auth == null || auth.isEmpty()) {
    37	            return defaultRegion;
    38	        }
    39	        Matcher matcher = CREDENTIAL_REGION_PATTERN.matcher(auth);
    40	        if (matcher.find()) {
    41	            return matcher.group(1);
    42	        }
    43	        return defaultRegion;
    44	    }
    45	
    46	    public String getDefaultRegion() {
    47	        return defaultRegion;
    48	    }
    49	
    50	    public String getAccountId() {
    51	        return defaultAccountId;
    52	    }
    53

    55	        return "arn:aws:" + service + ":" + region + ":" + defaultAccountId + ":" + resource;

#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cd /testbed
PORT=${PORT:-4566}
BASE="http://localhost:${PORT}"
LOG=/tmp/floci-repro-${PORT}.log
PIDFILE=/tmp/floci-repro-${PORT}.pid
rm -f "$LOG" "$PIDFILE"
cleanup() {
  if [[ -f "$PIDFILE" ]]; then
    kill "$(cat "$PIDFILE")" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
    wait "$(cat "$PIDFILE")" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
  fi
}
trap cleanup EXIT
java -jar target/quarkus-app/quarkus-run.jar >"$LOG" 2>&1 &
echo $! > "$PIDFILE"
for i in $(seq 1 120); do
  if curl -sf "$BASE/_floci/health" >/dev/null; then break; fi
  sleep 0.5
  if ! kill -0 "$(cat "$PIDFILE")" 2>/dev/null; then
    echo "server exited" >&2; cat "$LOG" >&2; exit 1
  fi
  if [[ $i -eq 120 ]]; then echo "server did not start" >&2; cat "$LOG" >&2; exit 1; fi
done
ZIP_B64=$(python3 - <<'PY'
import base64, io, zipfile
buf = io.BytesIO()
with zipfile.ZipFile(buf, 'w') as z:
    z.writestr('bootstrap', '#!/bin/sh\necho ok\n')
print(base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue()).decode())
PY
)

create_payload=$(python3 - <<PY

PY

  -H "Authorization: $AUTH" -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \
  -d "$update_payload" >/tmp/repro_update.json

for path in ['/tmp/repro_update.json','/tmp/repro_get.json']:

🎬 ACTION
cat > /tmp/repro_lambda_last_update_status.sh <<'EOF'
#!/usr/bin/env bash
set -euo pipefail
cd /testbed
PORT=${PORT:-4566}
BASE="http://localhost:${PORT}"
LOG=/tmp/floci-repro-${PORT}.log
PIDFILE=/tmp/floci-repro-${PORT}.pid
rm -f "$LOG" "$PIDFILE"
cleanup() {
  if [[ -f "$PIDFILE" ]]; then
    local pid
    pid=$(cat "$PIDFILE")
    kill "$pid" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
    wait "$pid" >/dev/null 2>&1 || true
  fi
}
trap cleanup EXIT
(
  cd /testbed/target/quarkus-app
  /usr/lib/jvm/java-25-openjdk-amd64/bin/java -jar quarkus-run.jar
) >"$LOG" 2>&1 &
echo $! > "$PIDFILE"
for i in $(seq 1 120); do
  if curl -sf "$BASE/_floci/health" >/dev/null; then break; fi
  sleep 0.5
  if ! kill -0 "$(cat "$PIDFILE")" 2>/dev/null; then
    echo "server exited" >&2; cat "$LOG" >&2; exit 1
  fi
  if [[ $i -eq 120 ]]; then echo "server did not start" >&2; cat "$LOG" >&2; exit 1; fi
done
ZIP_B64=$(python3 - <<'PY'
import base64, io, zipfile
buf = io.BytesIO()
with zipfile.ZipFile(buf, 'w') as z:
    z.writestr('bootstrap', '#!/bin/sh\necho ok\n')
print(base64.b64encode(buf.getvalue()).decode())
PY
)
AUTH='AWS4-HMAC-SHA256 Credential=test/20240530/us-east-1/lambda/aws4_request, SignedHeaders=host;x-amz-date, Signature=00'
create_payload=$(python3 - <<PY
import json
print(json.dumps({
  "FunctionName":"test-func",
  "Runtime":"provided.al2",
  "Handler":"bootstrap",
  "Role":"arn:aws:iam::000000000000:role/test",
  "Code":{"ZipFile":"$ZIP_B64"}
}))
PY
)
update_payload=$(python3 - <<PY
import json
print(json.dumps({"ZipFile":"$ZIP_B64"}))
PY
)
curl -sf -X POST "$BASE/2015-03-31/functions" \
  -H "Authorization: $AUTH" -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \
  -d "$create_payload" >/tmp/repro_create.json
curl -sf -X PUT "$BASE/2015-03-31/functions/test-func/code" \
  -H "Authorization: $AUTH" -H 'Content-Type: application/json' \
  -d "$update_payload" >/tmp/repro_update.json
curl -sf "$BASE/2015-03-31/functions/test-func" \
  -H "Authorization: $AUTH" >/tmp/repro_get.json
curl -sf "$BASE/2015-03-31/functions/test-func/configuration" \
  -H "Authorization: $AUTH" >/tmp/repro_get_config.json
python3 - <<'PY'
import json, sys
for path in ['/tmp/repro_update.json','/tmp/repro_get.json','/tmp/repro_get_config.json']:
    data=json.load(open(path))
    cfg=data.get('Configuration', data)
    print(path, 'LastUpdateStatus=', repr(cfg.get('LastUpdateStatus')), 'Reason=', repr(cfg.get('LastUpdateStatusReason')))
    if cfg.get('LastUpdateStatus') != 'Successful':
        print('BUG: expected LastUpdateStatus Successful in', path, 'got', repr(cfg.get('LastUpdateStatus')), file=sys.stderr)
        sys.exit(2)
    if cfg.get('LastUpdateStatusReason') != 'The function was successfully updated':
        print('BUG: expected LastUpdateStatusReason in', path, 'got', repr(cfg.get('LastUpdateStatusReason')), file=sys.stderr)
        sys.exit(3)
PY
EOF
chmod +x /tmp/repro_lambda_last_update_status.sh
/tmp/repro_lambda_last_update_status.sh
